# Dune Docs - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/home#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=8344ffbb623f6875145727e13925a620)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=54f1a9a73ae8fe5ec0235a2e52f9b870)](https://dune.com/)

Dune Docs

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[API Reference](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[SQL Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Resources](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview)

On this page

*   [Products](https://docs.dune.com/home#products)
    
*   [APIs & Connectors](https://docs.dune.com/home#apis-%26-connectors)
    
*   [Use Cases](https://docs.dune.com/home#use-cases)
    
*   [Resources](https://docs.dune.com/home#resources)
    

Our mission is to make crypto data accessible. We provide the infrastructure, data, and tools so your team can focus on insights and products, not wrangling data pipelines. With 100+ blockchains indexed, 3+ petabytes of data, and battle-tested by 1,500+ paying customers, Dune is your onchain data warehouse. Whether you’re building dashboards, powering applications, streaming data to your existing warehouse, or running transformation pipelines, any time you need to read aggregated data from the blockchain, Dune can serve it.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/home#products)

Products
----------------------------------------------------

Dune offers multiple products to meet your data needs, whether you’re building dashboards, powering applications, need a data warehouse, or integrating onchain data into your warehouse.

[Analytics Hub\
-------------\
\
Query, visualize, and share blockchain data with our web-based SQL editor and dashboard builder](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Datashare\
---------\
\
Stream Dune’s blockchain data directly to Snowflake, BigQuery, or Databricks](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Sim (Realtime APIs)\
-------------------\
\
Build applications with sub-second latency APIs for balances, transactions, and DeFi positions](https://docs.sim.dune.com/)
[Catalyst\
--------\
\
Dune’s blockchain integration toolkit for chains and protocols](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/home#apis-&-connectors)

APIs & Connectors

Beyond the core products, Dune offers APIs and connectors that extend how you can access and work with blockchain data programmatically.

[Analytics API\
-------------\
\
Execute queries, retrieve results, and manage data programmatically.](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/api-overview)
[dbt Connector\
-------------\
\
Build production data pipelines with dbt on Dune.](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/connectors/dbt/overview)
[External BI Tools\
-----------------\
\
Connect to Hex, Metabase, DBeaver, PowerBI, and other BI tools you already use to query Dune data.](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/connectors/trino/overview)

For a detailed comparison of products, data freshness, and pricing, see the [Products Overview](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison)
 page.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/home#use-cases)

Use Cases
------------------------------------------------------

Explore how teams use Dune to solve real business problems.

[Analytics\
---------\
\
Query, visualize, and analyze blockchain data for protocols, trading, and ecosystems**For:** Protocols, L1s, L2s, Appchains, Trading Teams, Researchers, VCs](https://docs.dune.com/docs/use-cases/analytics)
[Engineering\
-----------\
\
Transform, model, and pipeline onchain data into your applications and workflows**For:** Data Engineers, Product Teams, App Developers](https://docs.dune.com/docs/use-cases/engineering)
[Accounting, Audit & AML\
-----------------------\
\
Transaction monitoring, reconciliation, and compliance workflows**For:** Finance Teams, Compliance, Auditors, Regulators](https://docs.dune.com/docs/use-cases/accounting-audit-aml)
[Stream to Your Warehouse\
------------------------\
\
Export blockchain data to Snowflake, BigQuery, or Databricks for unified analytics**For:** Data Engineers, Data Scientists, Analytics Teams](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Transform Your Data\
-------------------\
\
Build production data pipelines and models with dbt on Dune**For:** Data Engineers, Data Scientists, Product Teams](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/connectors/dbt/overview)
[Build Wallet Applications\
-------------------------\
\
Power wallets, portfolio trackers, and DeFi apps with realtime blockchain data**For:** Developers, Product Teams, dApp Builders](https://docs.sim.dune.com/)

[​](https://docs.dune.com/home#resources)

# Data Catalog - Dune Docs

Data Catalog

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[API Reference](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[SQL Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Resources](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview)

On this page

*   [Blockchain Data](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#blockchain-data)
    
*   [EVM Chains](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#evm-chains)
    
*   [Other Chains](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#other-chains)
    
*   [Adding new blockchains](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#adding-new-blockchains)
    
*   [Curated](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#curated)
    
*   [Community Data](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#community-data)
    
*   [Our Data Difference](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#our-data-difference)
    

Our data catalog can be divided into the following categories:

*   [Blockchain Data](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#blockchain-data)
    *   [EVM-Compatible Chains](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#evm-compatible-chains)
        
    *   [Other chains](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#other-chains)
        
*   [Curated Data](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#curated)
    *   dex trades
    *   nft trades
    *   labels
    *   etc.
*   [Community Data](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#community-data)
    *   farcaster
    *   hyperliquid
    *   lens protocol
    *   snapshot
    *   reservoir
    *   etc.

Our entire data catalog is accessible through the Dune [Web App](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
, the [Dune API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
 or the [Snowflake Data Marketplace](https://app.snowflake.com/marketplace/providers/GZSVZMYSCO/Dune)
.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#blockchain-data)

Blockchain Data
===================================================================================

Dune provides data for a wide range of blockchains. Our data catalog includes raw data, decoded data, and abstracted data tables for each blockchain.

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#evm-chains)

EVM Chains

We provide the most comprehensive data catalog for Ethereum Mainnet and EVM-compatible rollups, sidechains and other layer 2 solutions. All EVM chains on Dune have raw data, decoded data and abstracted data tables available.

[Raw data\
--------](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/ethereum/raw/transactions)
[Decoded data\
------------](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/ethereum/decoded/overview)
[Curated data\
------------](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/curated/overview)

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#other-chains)

Other Chains

We provide data for a wide range of blockchains. The depth of data available for these chains may vary, but we always carry the full chain history in its raw form.

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#adding-new-blockchains)

Adding new blockchains

If you are a representative of a blockchain you would like to see supported on Dune, please reach out to us. We are always looking to expand our data catalog and provide the most comprehensive data available.

[Request a new blockchain integration!](https://dune.com/enterprise)

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#curated)

Curated
===================================================================

Dune provides a wide range of curated tables that simplify the process of querying and analyzing blockchain data. These tables are built on top of raw and decoded data tables and provide a high-level view of the data.

[Curated Data\
------------\
\
Curated data simplifies the process of querying and analyzing blockchain data.](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/curated/overview)

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#community-data)

Community Data
=================================================================================

Dune also carries off-chain data important to the web3 ecosystem that is provided by third-party data providers.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview#our-data-difference)

Our Data Difference
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We are building world-class data infrastructure so you don’t have to. Our data catalog is designed to provide the most comprehensive and accurate blockchain data available. We are committed to delivering the highest quality data, with the following features:

*   **Comprehensive Chain Histories:** Full access to blockchain data histories without gaps, ensuring source integrity.
*   **Accurate and Validated Data:** Commitment to accuracy, with validated consistency and uniqueness for all transactions and events.
*   **Rich Data Variety:** Decoded data transforms complex byte arrays into clear, structured, and usable information.
*   **Curated Data:** Dune’s [Curated Data Sets](https://github.com/duneanalytics/spellbook)
     enable collaborative, community-driven data modeling, unlocking new insights at lightning speed.
*   **Vibrant Community Data Pools:** Access to vast pools of data contributed by an active and innovative community.
*   **Cross-Chain:** Our entire data catalog is hosted in the same database, making it easy to compare and contrast data across different chains.

Credits & Billing

Overview

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[API Reference](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)

On this page

*   [What are credits?](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#what-are-credits)

*   [Important Notes](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#important-notes)
    

Dune’s operations largely rely on a credit system. This guide will explain the concept of credits, their consumption, and management.

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#what-are-credits)

What are credits?

Credits are the key to accessing a wide range of functions on the Dune platform. Whether you’re delving into writing queries or simply exploring dashboards, knowing how credits operate is crucial.

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#why-are-credits-important)

Why are credits important?

All actions on Dune, from refreshing a dashboard to exporting data via the API, consume credits. It’s vital for every user, viewer, or creator alike, to be mindful of their credit usage.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#your-credit-allocation)

Your Credit Allocation
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

No worries, every Dune user gets a monthly credit allowance. Here’s how it works:

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#%F0%9F%8E%9F%EF%B8%8F-monthly-credit-allowance)

🎟️ Monthly Credit Allowance

*   **Set Number of Credits:** Each month, your subscription plan provides a set allotment of credits.
*   **Top-Up:** Run out of credits? Our “pay as you go” option lets you add more anytime, ensuring your work is always in flow.

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#%F0%9F%94%84-rollover-policy)

🔄 Rollover Policy

*   **Monthly Refresh:** Credits reset at the start of each billing cycle; they do not roll over to the next month.
*   **Maximize Use:** Plan your activities to maximize the utility of your credits.

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#%F0%9F%91%A5-team-accounts)

👥 Team Accounts

*   **Collective Pool:** All team members draw from a shared pot of credits. Sync up to make the most of your resources.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#understanding-credit-use-on-dune)

Understanding Credit Use on Dune
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Credits power your work on Dune, and here’s how they’re typically used:

[Queries\
-------\
\
Running and creating queries consumes credits, with the amount varying based on complexity.](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/query-editor/query-window)
[Engine Power\
------------\
\
Larger tasks consume more computational resources, which increases credit usage based on actual compute used.](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/query-executions#query-engine-size)
[Refreshes\
---------\
\
Refreshing dashboards or widgets consumes credits; exact numbers are displayed contextually.](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/dashboards#keeping-your-dashboard-up-to-date)
[Exports\
-------\
\
Exporting data costs credits, with higher amounts for larger exports. Estimates are provided beforehand.](https://docs.dune.com/learning/how-tos/export-data-out)
[Auto-Runs\
---------\
\
Scheduling queries to run regularly consumes credits each time, with details available in the setup options.](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/query-editor/query-scheduler)

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#estimating-credit-usage)

Estimating Credit Usage

Understanding how your activities on Dune consume credits can help you manage your resources more effectively:

*   **Credit Estimates:** Always check for tooltips or on-screen indicators that provide real-time estimates of credit costs before you perform actions.
*   **Active Monitoring:** Keep a regular tab on your credit usage through your settings dashboard to avoid surprises.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#managing-your-credits)

Managing Your Credits
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#tracking-your-usage)

Tracking Your Usage

Hover over the odometer icon in your navigation bar for a quick glance at your credits. Make sure you’re looking at the right account context.

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#detailed-credit-information)

Detailed Credit Information

Go to **Settings** → **Subscriptions** for a deeper dive into your credit usage and options.

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#handling-excess-usage)

Handling Excess Usage

Exceeding your monthly allocation? Here’s how to handle it:

1.  Add a payment method to your account to use additional credits at a fee above your included limit.
2.  Set a cap in the **limit extra credits** field to keep your spending in check.

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#%F0%9F%93%8A-export-credit-usage-data)

📊 Export Credit Usage Data

Teams and users can export detailed credit usage metrics to analyze consumption patterns and optimize their Dune usage.

#### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#how-to-export-usage-data)

How to Export Usage Data

1.  Navigate to your team’s usage dashboard
2.  Click the **“Export usage”** button
3.  Your team’s last 30 days of usage data will be downloaded as a CSV file

#### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#understanding-the-exported-data)

Understanding the Exported Data

The exported CSV file contains comprehensive usage information with the following columns:

| Column | Description |
| --- | --- |
| timestamp | The exact date and time when the credit was consumed |
| user\_id | Unique identifier for the user who consumed the credits |
| user\_name | Display name of the user |
| service | The Dune service that consumed credits (e.g., query execution, API calls) |
| record\_type | Type of usage record |
| credit\_cost | Number of credits consumed for this action |
| plan | Your team’s current subscription plan |
| skipped\_quota\_enforcement | Indicates if quota limits were bypassed (true/false) |
| query\_id | Unique identifier for queries (when applicable) |
| metadata | Additional contextual information about the usage |

#### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#use-cases-for-exported-data)

Use Cases for Exported Data

The exported usage data enables teams to: • **Track individual user consumption:** Identify which team members are using the most credits  
• **Analyze service usage patterns:** Understand which Dune services consume the most credits  
• **Budget planning:** Use historical data to forecast future credit needs  
• **Optimize queries:** Identify expensive queries using the query\_id field  
• **Compliance and reporting:** Generate usage reports for internal auditing  
• **Cost allocation:** Distribute costs across different teams or projects based on actual usage

#### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#data-analysis-tips)

Data Analysis Tips

• Import the CSV into spreadsheet software or data analysis tools  
• Create pivot tables to summarize usage by user, service, or time period  
• Use the timestamp field to analyze usage patterns over time  
• Filter by query\_id to identify and optimize resource-intensive queries  
• Monitor the credit\_cost column to track spending trends

#### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview#important-notes)

Important Notes

• The export includes the last 30 days of data  
• All timestamps are in UTC  
• Credit costs reflect your team’s pricing plan at the time of usage  
• The metadata field may contain additional JSON-formatted information depending on the service

Was this page helpful?

Query Engine

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)

[SQL Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Resources](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview)

On this page

*   [Key Features](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview#key-features)
    
*   [DuneSQL Essentials](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview#dunesql-essentials)
    
*   [Debugging](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview#debugging)
    

New to DuneSQL? Watch our [DuneSQL overview video](https://docs.dune.com/resources/learning/video-tutorials#dunesql-overview)
 for a quick introduction.

DuneSQL enhances blockchain data analysis by leveraging a Trino fork. This engine excels in performance for interactive queries across vast datasets, from gigabytes to petabytes.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview#key-features)

Key Features
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

DuneSQL shines with unique blockchain-focused capabilities:

*   **Varbinary Data Types**: Store blockchain specifics like addresses and hashes efficiently.
*   **Uint256 & Int256 Support**: Essential for blockchain’s large numerical data.
*   **Columnar Storage**: Optimizes read speed by organizing data by columns.
*   **Query Views**: Enables complex query construction and reusability.
*   **Materialized Views**: For enhanced query performance through pre-computed results.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview#dunesql-essentials)

DuneSQL Essentials
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

DuneSQL offers a robust platform for blockchain data exploration. As a modified version of TrinoSQL, it supports scalable, interactive analysis across diverse data sizes. Our documentation equips you with the necessary tools to efficiently harness DuneSQL.

[Functions and Operators\
-----------------------\
\
DuneSQL’s syntax toolbox.](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/Functions-and-operators)
[Data Types\
----------\
\
Understanding DuneSQL data formats.](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/datatypes)
[Reserved Keywords\
-----------------\
\
Keywords off-limits for naming.](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/reserved-keywords)
[Writing Efficient Queries\
-------------------------\
\
Strategies for query optimization.](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/writing-efficient-queries)
[Querying a Query\
----------------\
\
Layer queries for complex insights.](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/query-a-query)
[Materialized Views\
------------------\
\
Boost query speed with stored views.](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/materialized-views)

[​](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview#debugging)

Debugging
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

Need help with DuneSQL? Start here:

*   Google `<problem> Trino SQL` for general inquiries.
*   Chat with your favorite AI assistant and ask for `Trino SQL` help.
*   Check [Trino’s official documentation](https://trino.io/docs/current/functions.html)
     for detailed insights.

Accounting, audit, and compliance teams depend on Dune for transaction monitoring, data reconciliation, financial reporting, and AML investigations across blockchain networks.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/use-cases/accounting-audit-aml#common-use-cases)

Common Use Cases
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Transaction Monitoring
----------------------

Track onchain transactions, wallet flows, and cross-chain movements for compliance

Account Reconciliation
----------------------

Verify token balances, staking positions, and DeFi holdings at any point in time

Financial Reporting
-------------------

Calculate realized gains/losses from DEX trades, staking rewards, and LP positions

Market Manipulation Detection
-----------------------------

Pump and dump analysis, wash trading on DEXs, prediction market wash trading, LP manipulation

AML & Fraud Investigation
-------------------------

Wallet clustering, sybil detection, sanctions screening, illicit fund tracing

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/use-cases/accounting-audit-aml#who-this-is-for)

Who This Is For
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Accounting & Finance
--------------------

Transaction monitoring, reconciliation, and financial reporting for crypto treasuries

Risk & Compliance
-----------------

AML/KYC workflows, sanctions screening, and regulatory compliance monitoring

Brokerages & Exchanges
----------------------

Trade reconciliation, compliance reporting, and market surveillance

Custodians
----------

Asset verification, balance audits, and custody reporting

Professional Services
---------------------

Big 4 auditors, tax preparers, and consulting firms serving crypto clients

Public Sector
-------------

Regulators, policymakers, and government agencies monitoring crypto markets

Data engineering teams use Dune to build production data pipelines, transform blockchain data, and integrate onchain insights into their applications and workflows.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/use-cases/engineering#common-use-cases)

Common Use Cases
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Build Data Pipelines
--------------------

Create production-grade data models and transformation pipelines with dbt on Dune

Stream to Your Warehouse
------------------------

Export blockchain data to Snowflake, BigQuery, or Databricks via Datashare

Programmatic Access
-------------------

Execute queries, manage data, and integrate Dune into your applications via Analytics API

Power Wallet & App Backends
---------------------------

Build realtime wallet experiences and DeFi apps with sub-second latency via Sim APIs

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/use-cases/engineering#who-this-is-for)

Who This Is For
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Data Engineering Teams
----------------------

Build and maintain data pipelines, models, and transformations on blockchain data

Wallets & Apps Engineering
--------------------------

Power wallet backends, portfolio trackers, and DeFi applications with onchain data

AI & Derived Analytics
----------------------

Build ML models, derived datasets, and AI-powered analytics on blockchain data

Product Teams
-------------

Integrate onchain data into product workflows, dashboards, and customer-facing features

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/use-cases/engineering#how-it-works)

How It Works
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Dune provides multiple products to power your data engineering workflows:

# Upload Data - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/upload-data#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=8344ffbb623f6875145727e13925a620)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=54f1a9a73ae8fe5ec0235a2e52f9b870)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Analytics Hub

Upload Data

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[API Reference](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[SQL Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Resources](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview)

On this page

*   [Querying for the data in Dune](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/upload-data#querying-for-the-data-in-dune)
    
*   [Updating data](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/upload-data#updating-data)
    
*   [Private data](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/upload-data#private-data)
    
*   [Deleting data](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/upload-data#deleting-data)
    
*   [Large Amounts of Data](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/upload-data#large-amounts-of-data)
    

**Easily upload your own data to Dune** This feature allows you to upload any csv file to Dune and query it like any other table in Dune. Currently, we only supports uploading CSV files with a maximum size of 200 MB. The app will return an error if the file size exceeds this limit.  
Additionally, column names in the table can’t start with a special character or digits. The files you upload will be queryable via the schema `dune.team_name.dataset_name`. For example, if you upload a file called `energy_data.csv` to the team `dune` and name the dataset `energy_data`, you will be able to query the data via `dune.dune.energy_data`. You’ll be able to query for your data in any query.

Copy

Ask AI

    Select * from dune.dune.dataset_energy_data
    

All data uploaded is public and can be accessed by anyone.  
Private data uploads are available only on **Enterprise plans.**

You can also upload data via the API. Check out the [API documentation](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/tables/endpoint/upload)
 for more information.

1.  Click on the “Upload Data” button in the menu of the Dune UI.
2.  Select the csv file you want to upload.
3.  Name your table and add a description.
4.  Click on save to finish the upload.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/upload-data#querying-for-the-data-in-dune)

Querying for the data in Dune
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once the data has been uploaded, you can explore it in the my data section in the data explorer: ![upload data](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/dune/web-app/web-app/images/upload_data.gif) You can query for your data in any query.

Copy

Ask AI

    Select * from dune.dune.dataset_energy_data
    

To check whether the datatypes are correctly inferred, you can check the table details in the [data explorer](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/query-editor/data-explorer)
.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/upload-data#updating-data)

Updating data
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Updating data is only possible via the [API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/quickstart/tables-eg)
. In the UI you can only replace the data with a new (updated) file that carries the same name. However, you can use the “query a query” feature to query multiple .csv files at once. **For example:**

Copy

Ask AI

    --query_2441513
    
    Select * from dune.dune.dataset_energy_data_1
    
    UNION ALL
    
    Select * from dune.dune.dataset_energy_data_2
    
    -- add more as it becomes relevant
    

In your main query, you could then simply refer to this query.

Copy

Ask AI

    Select * from ethereum.transactions t
    left join query_2441513 q on q.address = t."from"
    

[​](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/upload-data#private-data)

Private data
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you don’t want to share your data with the world, you can also upload private data. Private data is only visible to you and your team members. To upload private data, **you need to be on an Enterprise plan**. If you are on an Enterprise plan, you can upload private data by toggling the “make table private” switch in the upload data modal. You can also change the privacy settings of a dataset after it has been uploaded. To do so, go to settings -> data page and click on the three dots next to the dataset you want to change the privacy settings for. Then click on “make table private” to make the table private or “make table public” to make it public.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/upload-data#deleting-data)

Deleting data
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can delete your data via your settings page.

1.  Click on the “settings” button in the menu of the Dune UI.
2.  Click on “data”.
3.  Find the dataset you want to delete.
4.  Click on the three dots to open the options for the dataset.
5.  Click on “delete dataset”.
6.  confirm the deletion.
7.  The dataset is now deleted.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/upload-data#large-amounts-of-data)

Large Amounts of Data
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want to share valuable off-chain data on Dune with your community, we are happy to discuss custom arrangements. Please reach indicate your interest via this [form](https://bit.ly/dune-data-integration)
. This is only applicable for datasets with positive externalities for the Dune community. Examples include:

*   [Farcaster](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/community/farcaster/overview)
    
*   [Reservoir](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/community/reservoir/overview)
    
*   [Flashbots](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/community/flashbots/overview)
    

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Raise issue](https://github.com/duneanalytics/dune-docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/web-app/upload-data)

[Okta SSO](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/okta-sso)
[Export Data Out of Dune](https://docs.dune.com/learning/how-tos/export-data-out)

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#product-updates)

Product updates
============================================================================

> New releases and improvements

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#december-2025)

December 2025

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#domain-restricted-google-sso-enterprise)

Domain-Restricted Google SSO (Enterprise)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Team admins can now enable domain restriction via Google SSO in team settings. This forces team members to log in using their company email (e.g., @company.com), preventing non-employees from accessing the workspace. When enabled, all team members are logged out and must re-authenticate with Google SSO. See the [Google SSO documentation](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/google-sso-domain-restriction)
 for setup details.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#okta-sso-enterprise)

Okta SSO (Enterprise)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We now support Okta SSO for Enterprise customers, a frequently requested feature for enterprise security requirements. You can enable Okta SSO via team settings under the new “Settings & Privacy” tab. We also extended this feature to support multiple domains for organizations with complex Okta tenant configurations. See the [Okta SSO documentation](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/okta-sso)
 for setup details.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#usage-table)

Usage Table
--------------------------------------------------------------------

A new Usage table is now available, containing records of metered App, API, and Connector events. Users can search, filter, and export these records for detailed usage analysis and cost tracking.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#private-content-by-default-enterprise)

Private Content by Default (Enterprise)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enterprise customers can now control the default privacy mode for team content with three options:

*   **Public by default** — Team members choose per content
*   **Private by default** — New content defaults to private, can be made public individually
*   **Private only** — All content forced private, external sharing disabled

This helps teams working with sensitive data ensure privacy is the default, making link sharing an explicit opt-in.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#improvements)

Improvements
----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Export CSV downloads** — Improved CSV export experience for usage data
*   **Folder filtering** — Filter by Dashboards or Queries inside folders
*   **Embed fix** — Fixed an issue where embeds did not show username/avatar when the query belonged to a user
*   **EVM Contract resubmission** — Resubmission actions (rename, upgrade, delete) now gated to paid team plans
*   **Query editor UX** — Click the drag icon to expand the query editor (in addition to dragging)

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#november-2025)

November 2025

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#databricks-support-for-datashare-enterprise)

Databricks Support for Datashare (Enterprise)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Datashare now supports Databricks, expanding our data warehouse integrations beyond Snowflake and BigQuery. Stream Dune’s complete blockchain dataset directly into your Databricks environment. See the [Databricks documentation](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-databricks)
 and read the [announcement blog post](https://dune.com/blog/expanding-dune-datashare-with-databricks)
.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#dbt-connector-enterprise)

dbt Connector (Enterprise)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enterprise customers can now use dbt for in-platform data transformations with incremental runs. Build production data pipelines, version control your models, and run transformations directly on Dune. See the [dbt Connector documentation](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/connectors/dbt/overview)
 and read the [announcement blog post](https://dune.com/blog/run-dbt-on-dune-your-crypto-data-warehouse)
.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#new-chain-support)

New Chain Support
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Added support for [Initia](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/initia/overview)
, [Kalshi](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/kalshi/overview)
, [Story](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/story/overview)
, [Mezo](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/mezo/overview)
, and [Monad](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/monad/overview)
. Explore raw, decoded, and curated data for these new chains in the Data Catalog.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#new-api-landing-page)

New API Landing Page
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A new [API landing page](https://dune.com/apis)
 provides a unified view of all endpoints with quick curl/preview actions and documentation links.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#new-api-endpoints)

New API Endpoints
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

New endpoints for executing arbitrary SQL, pipeline executions, usage data, and dataset metadata. See the [API documentation](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
 for details.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/changelog#improvements-2)

Improvements
------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Improved usage overview** — Charts and copyable API keys for better visibility
*   **Increased max query result size** — From 8GB to 32GB
*   **Restructured [API documentation](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
    ** — Scannable for newcomers while keeping advanced details discoverable
*   **Updated SDKs** — All new endpoints included
*   **Deprecated `/v1/tables` endpoints** — Moved to `/v1/uploads`. See the [Tables API documentation](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/tables/endpoint/overview)
     for migration details

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/learning/video-tutorials#getting-started-with-dune)

Getting Started with Dune
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These videos will help you get up and running with Dune quickly, understanding how data flows through the platform and how to navigate the app effectively.

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/learning/video-tutorials#dune-official-getting-started-series)

Dune Official Getting Started Series

Learn how the data flows and how to navigate the Dune app to create queries, visualizations, and dashboards. This comprehensive playlist covers all the essentials you need to get started.

[View the full playlist on YouTube →](https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLK3b5d4iK10ext4v-GBySekaA8-GP8quD)

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/learning/video-tutorials#becoming-a-crypto-data-analyst)

Becoming a Crypto Data Analyst

Ready to level up? Follow the crypto data analyst roadmap to build your skills and establish yourself as an expert in blockchain analytics.

* * *

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/learning/video-tutorials#writing-&-running-queries)

Writing & Running Queries
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Master the Query Editor and DuneSQL to construct powerful queries for blockchain data analysis.

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/learning/video-tutorials#query-editor-walkthrough)

Query Editor Walkthrough

The Query Editor is where you’ll spend most of your time on Dune. Learn how to use its features effectively, including autocomplete, running query selections, and using keyboard shortcuts.

**Related docs:** [Writing Queries](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/query-editor/query-window)

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/learning/video-tutorials#dunesql-overview)

DuneSQL Overview

DuneSQL is a Trino fork fine-tuned for blockchain analytics. Learn about its key features including varbinary data types, uint256 support, columnar storage, and materialized views.

**Related docs:** [Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)

* * *

[​](https://docs.dune.com/resources/learning/video-tutorials#finding-&-understanding-data)

Explore Dune’s comprehensive data catalog to find blockchain data, curated datasets, and community data. This video covers how to browse categories, filter tables, and preview data.

, [Finding Tables](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/query-editor/data-explorer)

# Products Overview - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=8344ffbb623f6875145727e13925a620)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=54f1a9a73ae8fe5ec0235a2e52f9b870)](https://dune.com/)

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Products Overview

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[API Reference](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[SQL Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Resources](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview)

On this page

*   [Capabilities](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison#capabilities)
    
*   [Query & Architecture](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison#query-%26-architecture)
    
*   [Data Coverage](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison#data-coverage)
    
*   [Interface & Pricing](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison#interface-%26-pricing)
    
*   [Quick Selection Guide](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison#quick-selection-guide)
    

Dune delivers blockchain data via three core products: **Analytics Hub**, **Datashare**, and **Sim (Realtime APIs)**. Each product serves different use cases, from ad-hoc analytics to real-time wallet application development.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison#capabilities)

Capabilities
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

What each product is best suited for.

|     | [Analytics Hub](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview) | [Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare) | [Sim (Realtime APIs)](https://sim.dune.com/) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Best For** | Primary onchain data warehouse, Analytic workflows, [Data transformations](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/connectors/dbt/overview) | Data warehouse integration & Interoperability | Build realtime wallets, portfolio apps |
| **SQL Access** | ✓ Full SQL | ✓ Full SQL | REST APIs |
| **Historical Data** | ✓ Full historical | ✓ Full historical | Realtime |
| **Authentication** | Dune account, API key | Warehouse credentials | Sim account, API key |

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison#query-&-architecture)

Query & Architecture
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How each product handles queries and processes data under the hood.

|     | [Analytics Hub](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview) | [Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare) | [Sim (Realtime APIs)](https://sim.dune.com/) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Query Infra** | DuneSQL / Trino | Snowflake, BigQuery, Databricks | N/A |
| **Query Speed** | ~3 seconds | N/A | N/A |
| **Engine** | Custom Trino (Small, Medium, Large) | N/A | N/A |
| **Architecture** | OLAP, Delta parquet | OLAP, mostly Iceberg parquet | Real-time |

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison#data-coverage)

Data Coverage
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

What data is available and how fresh it is across each product.

|     | [Analytics Hub](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview) | [Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare) | [Sim (Realtime APIs)](https://sim.dune.com/) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Freshness** | EVM: ~1-15 min  <br>Solana: ~1-5 min  <br>Curated: ~1 hour | Hourly or daily | < 1 second |
| **Blockchains** | [100+ chains](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/overview) | [100+ chains](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/overview) | 60+ chains |
| **Schemas** | [Raw](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/ethereum/raw/transactions)<br>, [Decoded](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/ethereum/decoded/overview)<br>, Curated ([DEX Trades](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/curated/dex-trades)<br>, [Prices](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/curated/prices)<br>, [Token Transfers](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/curated/token-transfers/overview)<br>, [more](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/curated/overview)<br>) | Same as Analytics Hub | Curated (Balances, Activity, DeFi, Token Info) |

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison#interface-&-pricing)

Interface & Pricing
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How you access each product and pricing.

|     | [Analytics Hub](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview) | [Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare) | [Sim (Realtime APIs)](https://sim.dune.com/) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Interface** | [Dune App](https://dune.com/)<br>, [Analytics API](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/api-overview)<br>, [External BI Tools](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/connectors/trino/overview) | [BigQuery](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-bigquery)<br>, [Snowflake](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-snowflake)<br>, [Databricks](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-databricks) | REST APIs |
| **Pricing** | Credits (compute-based) | Flat Subscription Fees | API Call Volume (CUs) |

* * *

[​](https://docs.dune.com/docs/product-comparison#quick-selection-guide)

Quick Selection Guide
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Analytics Hub\
-------------\
\
**Best for:** Your primary onchain data warehouse, analytic workflows, and data transformationsFull SQL access with 100+ chains, flexible schemas, and compute-based pricing](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/overview)
[Datashare\
---------\
\
**Best for:** Data warehouse integration and interoperabilityDirect access via Snowflake, BigQuery, or Databricks with full historical data](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare)
[Sim (Realtime APIs)\
-------------------\
\
**Best for:** Building realtime wallets, portfolio trackers, and DeFi applicationsSub-second response times with 60+ chains via REST APIs](https://sim.dune.com/)
[Catalyst\
--------\
\
**Best for:** Blockchain integration and data infrastructureDune’s toolkit for chains and protocols to get indexed and make their data accessible](https://docs.dune.com/catalyst/overview)

**Why is Catalyst not in the comparison tables?** Catalyst is Dune’s blockchain integration toolkit designed for chains and protocols, not end-user data consumption. It powers how blockchains get indexed into Dune rather than how users query data, so it serves a fundamentally different purpose than Analytics Hub, Datashare, and Sim (Realtime APIs).

[Sim (Realtime APIs)](https://docs.dune.com/docs/sim-real-time-apis)

Test Dune’s blockchain data on your preferred platform:

Snowflake Trial
---------------

**Self-service** - Available now

*   100+ chains, 30-day free trial
*   Via Snowflake Marketplace

[Get Started →](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-trial#snowflake)

BigQuery Trial
--------------

**Custom setup** - Contact required

*   100+ chains in US/EU regions
*   Email for trial access

[Request Access →](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-trial#bigquery)

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-trial#snowflake)

Snowflake
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to [Dune on Snowflake Marketplace](https://app.snowflake.com/marketplace/providers/GZSVZMYSCO/Dune)
    
2.  Click “Get” on any dataset for 30-day trial
3.  Configure database name and roles
4.  Start querying

You may need to click “Get” twice - once to copy data, then again to add to your Snowflake.

See [Snowflake guide](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-snowflake)
 for data types and query examples.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-trial#bigquery)

BigQuery
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

Email [\[email protected\]](https://docs.dune.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#41252035203229203324326c32202d24320125342f246f222e2c)
 or use our [Enterprise form](https://dune.com/enterprise)
 **Include:**

*   GCP Project ID
*   Preferred region (US Central 1 or EU West 2)
*   Chains of interest

We’ll set up trial access in your BigQuery project with technical support. See [BigQuery guide](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-bigquery)
 for data types and query examples.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-trial#support)

# Datashare Overview - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=8344ffbb623f6875145727e13925a620)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=54f1a9a73ae8fe5ec0235a2e52f9b870)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Dune Datashare

Datashare Overview

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[API Reference](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[SQL Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Resources](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview)

On this page

*   [How Datashare Works](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#how-datashare-works)
    
*   [Platforms](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#platforms)
    
*   [Why Choose Datashare](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#why-choose-datashare)
    
*   [Working with Dune](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#working-with-dune)
    
*   [Getting Started](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#getting-started)
    
*   [What We Need From You](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#what-we-need-from-you)
    
*   [Setup Process](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#setup-process)
    
*   [Platform-Specific Access](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#platform-specific-access)
    
*   [Next Steps](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#next-steps)
    

Datashare brings our complete blockchain dataset (1.5M+ tables, 100+ chains) directly into your data warehouse. Query blockchain data in your own environment with complete privacy and control.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#how-datashare-works)

How Datashare Works
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Datashare replicates Dune’s processed blockchain data directly into your cloud data warehouse: ![Datashare Architecture](https://mintcdn.com/dune/7jTylmCpqk1GQLzb/datashare/images/datashare-architecture.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=7jTylmCpqk1GQLzb&q=85&s=41a20faaabb6076ec3fe37f3b90b7bdf)

1.  **Data Replication**: We maintain live copies of all Dune tables in your Snowflake or BigQuery environment
2.  **Native Integration**: Data appears as regular tables/datasets in your warehouse - no APIs or external connections
3.  **Fresh Data**: Automatic updates keep your data in sync with Dune’s platform (hourly/daily refresh)
4.  **Your Environment**: Query using your warehouse’s native SQL, compute, and security controls

This is the same curated, decoded blockchain data that powers dune.com - optimized for analytics with proper data types and indexing.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#platforms)

Platforms
---------------------------------------------------------------------

| **Platform** | **Access Method** | **Trial Available** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ❄️ **[Snowflake](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-snowflake)<br>** | Marketplace or Direct Share | 30-day free trial |
| 🔍 **[BigQuery](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-bigquery)<br>** | Dataset Sharing | Contact for trial |

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#why-choose-datashare)

Why Choose Datashare
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Complete Privacy**: Query in your warehouse - Dune never sees your queries or results
*   **Join Your Data**: Seamlessly combine blockchain data with your internal datasets
*   **Cost Control**: Use your existing warehouse compute and manage costs directly
*   **No Rate Limits**: Query as much as you need without API constraints
*   **Enterprise Security**: Leverage your warehouse’s existing security and compliance controls

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#working-with-dune)

Working with Dune
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#getting-started)

Getting Started

**For Trials:**

*   **Snowflake**: Self-service via [Snowflake Marketplace](https://app.snowflake.com/marketplace/providers/GZSVZMYSCO/Dune)
    
*   **BigQuery**: Email [\[email protected\]](https://docs.dune.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#593d382d382a31382b3c2a742a38353c2a193d2c373c773a3634)
     with your requirements

**For Production:** Contact our enterprise team at [dune.com/enterprise](https://dune.com/enterprise)
 or [\[email protected\]](https://docs.dune.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#91f5f0e5f0e2f9f0e3f4e2bce2f0fdf4e2d1f5e4fff4bff2fefc)

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#what-we-need-from-you)

What We Need From You

To set up datashare access, we need specific identifiers from your cloud environment:

Snowflake Requirements

Please provide your Snowflake data sharing account identifier so I can grant you access to a listing. To find this identifier log in to your Snowflake account and click at your user profile at the bottom of the screen > _Account_ > _View account details_ > Copy data sharing account identifier (you can view a visual path [here](https://docs.snowflake.com/en/alias/client/account-identifier-listing)
). You can also run the following SQL command:

Copy

Ask AI

    SELECT CURRENT_ORGANIZATION_NAME() || '.' || CURRENT_ACCOUNT_NAME();
    

Then, share your identifier with me.

BigQuery Requirements

**Required Information:**

*   **GCP Project ID** (not project name - the unique ID)
*   **Principal for access** (user email, service account, or domain)
*   **Preferred region** (US Central 1 or EU West 2)
*   **Chains of interest** (optional - we can share all by default)

**Principal Examples:**

*   User: `user:[[email protected]](https://docs.dune.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) `
*   Service Account: `serviceAccount:[[email protected]](https://docs.dune.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) `
*   Domain: `domain:company.com` (all users in domain)

### 

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#setup-process)

Setup Process

1.  **Share Identifiers**: Provide the required identifiers for your platform
2.  **Access Configuration**: We configure sharing permissions on our side
3.  **Verification**: We’ll confirm when data is available in your environment
4.  **Support**: Ongoing technical support for queries and optimization

**Security Note**: We only need identifiers to grant access - never passwords, keys, or other sensitive credentials.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#platform-specific-access)

Platform-Specific Access
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Snowflake Guide\
---------------\
\
Marketplace access, data types, and query examples](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-snowflake)
[BigQuery Guide\
--------------\
\
Dataset sharing, principals, and optimization tips](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-bigquery)

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#next-steps)

Next Steps
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **[Try a free trial](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-trial)
    ** - Test our data on your platform
2.  **[Review platform guides](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-snowflake)
    ** - Learn about data types and querying
3.  **[Contact enterprise team](https://dune.com/enterprise)
    ** - Discuss production requirements
4.  **[Check FAQs](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-faqs)
    ** - Common questions and troubleshooting

Need a different platform or have questions? [Contact us](https://dune.com/enterprise)
 or email [\[email protected\]](https://docs.dune.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#9feceaefeff0edebdffbeaf1fab1fcf0f2)
.

Databricks Integration
==========================================================================================================

Access Dune’s comprehensive blockchain data directly in your Databricks environment.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-databricks#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Databricks integration allows you to:

*   Query Dune data using Databricks SQL
*   Build ML pipelines with blockchain data
*   Integrate with your existing Databricks workflows

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-databricks#getting-started)

Getting Started
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Contact the Dune team to enable Databricks access
2.  Configure your Databricks workspace
3.  Connect to Dune’s data catalog

[​](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare-databricks#use-cases)

Use Cases
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Machine learning on blockchain data
*   Advanced analytics and data science
*   Integration with existing Databricks pipelines

# henesys.logs_decoded - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/logs-decoded#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=8344ffbb623f6875145727e13925a620)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=54f1a9a73ae8fe5ec0235a2e52f9b870)](https://dune.com/)

Decoded

henesys.logs\_decoded

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[API Reference](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[SQL Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Resources](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview)

Table Description
-----------------

The `logs_decoded` table contains decoded logs from henesys transactions. The table matches `topic0` to the event signature and the corresponding event name. The table does not contain the full event data and is not suitable for analysis of smart contract level data. For that, use the specific event tables as described in [Event Logs](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs)
.This table is great for gaining a high level understanding of the types of events that are being emitted by a smart contract or smart contracts of a certain protocol.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

# henesys.event_logs - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs#content-area)

Decoded

henesys.event\_logs

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[API Reference](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[SQL Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Resources](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview)

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs#overview)
    
*   [Event Logs in Dune](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs#event-logs-in-dune)
    
*   [Example](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs#example)
    
*   [Multiple Instances](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs#multiple-instances)
    
*   [Further Reading](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs#further-reading)
    

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs#overview)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Smart contracts emit event logs when certain predefined actions are completed. The emitted event logs are stored on the blockchain and are publicly accessible. Event logs are an important tool for smart contract developers to communicate with the outside world, as well as for data analysts to keep track of what happens inside of a smart contract. For example, the ERC20 standard defines the `Transfer` event, which is emitted every time a token transfer occurs. The event log contains the sender, the recipient and the amount of tokens transferred.

Copy

Ask AI

    event Transfer(address indexed from, address indexed to, uint256 value);
    

Decoded event logs always originate from the fields `topic0`, `topic1`, `topic2`, `topic3` and `data` in the `logs` table.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs#event-logs-in-dune)

Event Logs in Dune
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In Dune, we store all event logs of decoded smart contracts in separate tables. The structure published in these logs is predefined by the developer of the smart contract, the content is dynamically created during the transaction. Logs are useful for monitoring, alerting and in general keeping track of what happens inside of a smart contract. Logs are your best friend as a data analyst since they reliably present you with data that is intended to be analyzed post factum. If you ever want to see which logs _can_ be emitted by a smart contract, you can simply search for the keyword `emit` in the source code of the smart contract. We will decode all event logs for smart contracts into tables named accordingly to this schema: `[projectname_blockchain].[contractName]_evt_[eventName]`

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs#example)

Example
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Let’s take the [uniswap v3 factory](https://etherscan.io/address/0x1f98431c8ad98523631ae4a59f267346ea31f984#code)
 as an example and look at the event that gets emitted upon the creation of a new pool. The event is called `PoolCreated` and gets emitted every time somebody successfully deploys a new Uniswap V3 pool by calling the function `createPool`. The event will readily give us information like the tokens in the pool, the fee tier of this pool and the tick spacing. In Etherscan, you can easily look at the event logs of transaction by opening the [logs tab](https://etherscan.io/tx/0xdeb368592f3de0f2840754bce61d2c3f29cdb3407c63c699052e68a854c71eaa#eventlog)
. In Dune, this particular event will be stored in the table: `uniswap_v3_ethereum.Factory_evt_PoolCreated`

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs#multiple-instances)

Multiple Instances
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If there is multiple instances of a contract we will collect all event logs across all instances of this smart contract in one table. For example, all uniswap v3 pool `swap` events (on ethereum) are stored in the table: `uniswap_v3_ethereum.Pair_evt_Swap` The column `contract_address` indicates as to which smart contract emitted this event.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs#further-reading)

Further Reading
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Understanding event logs on the Ethereum blockchain](https://medium.com/mycrypto/understanding-event-logs-on-the-ethereum-blockchain-f4ae7ba50378)
    
*   [Everything You Ever Wanted to Know About Events and Logs on Ethereum](https://medium.com/linum-labs/everything-you-ever-wanted-to-know-about-events-and-logs-on-ethereum-fec84ea7d0a5)
    

[Submit any contract for decoding\
--------------------------------](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/decoding/decoding-contracts)
[Explore already decoded contracts\
---------------------------------](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/ethereum/decoded/contracts)

henesys.traces\_decoded

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)

Table Description
-----------------

The `traces_decoded` table contains decoded traces from henesys transactions. The table matches `MethodID`, which consists of the first 4 bytes of any eth call, to the trace signature and the corresponding Method name. The table does not contain the full trace data and is not suitable for analysis of smart contract level data. For that, use the specific event tables as described in [Call-tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/traces-decoded)
.This table is great for gaining a high level understanding of the types of events that are being emitted by a smart contract or smart contracts of a certain protocol.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

# Henesys Decoded Overview - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/overview#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=8344ffbb623f6875145727e13925a620)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=54f1a9a73ae8fe5ec0235a2e52f9b870)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Decoded

Henesys Decoded Overview

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[API Reference](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[SQL Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Resources](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview)

Overview of Dune's Decoded Data Approach
----------------------------------------

Dune uses the ABI (Application Binary Interface) of smart contracts to decode blockchain transactions into structured tables. Each event log and function call from the ABI are parsed into their own tables. This decoding process transforms the raw, encoded data on the blockchain into human-readable tables, simplifying the analysis of smart contract data.Dune's decoded data approach offers several benefits:

*   **Enhanced Readability:** The decoded data tables provide a clear and intuitive representation of smart contract activities.
*   **Efficient Analysis:** The structured tables enable efficient querying and analysis of smart contract data.
*   **Handling Multiple Contract Instances:** For smart contracts with multiple instances, Dune aggregates the data from these instances into a single table, simplifying the analysis process.
*   **Collaborative Mapping:** Dune's smart contract library is continuously expanded through the active participation of the Dune community, ensuring that the decoding coverage remains comprehensive and current.

[Explore decoded logs\
--------------------](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/event-logs)
[Explore decoded traces\
----------------------](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/call-tables)

Which contracts have decoded data?
----------------------------------

Contract submission on Dune are driven by the community. Usually, the odds are good that the contract you are looking at is already decoded, but especially for new projects or new contracts, it might be that the contract is not decoded yet. In those cases, you can submit the contract to be decoded. Decoding usually takes about 24 hours, in special cases it might take longer.You can check if contracts are already decoded by querying the `[blockchain].contracts` tables, the [data explorer](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/query-editor/data-explorer)
, or use [this dashboard](https://dune.com/dune/is-my-contract-decoded-yet-v2)
.

[Submit any contract for decoding\
--------------------------------](https://docs.dune.com/web-app/decoding-contracts)
[Explore already decoded contracts\
---------------------------------](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/contracts)

How does decoding work?
-----------------------

Smart Contracts on any EVM blockchain are mostly written in high-level languages like [Solidity](https://docs.soliditylang.org/en/v0.8.2)
 or [Vyper](https://vyper.readthedocs.io/en/stable)
. In order for them to be deployed to an EVM execution environment, they need to be compiled to EVM executable bytecode. Once deployed, the bytecode gets associated with an address on the respective chain and is permanently stored in the chain's state storage.To be able to interact with this smart contract, which is now just bytecode, we need a guide to call the functions defined in the high-level languages. This translation of names and arguments into byte representation is done using an **Application Binary Interface (ABI)**. The ABI documents names, types, and arguments precisely, which allows us to interact with the smart contract using a somewhat human-readable format. The ABI can be compiled using the high-level language source code.**The ABI is used to call a smart contract or interpret the data it emits.**![Decoding process illustration](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/images/decoding.png)

Decoding Example
----------------

We are going to look at an event log of an ERC20 transfer event from the [smart contract](https://etherscan.io/token/0x429881672B9AE42b8EbA0E26cD9C73711b891Ca5#readContract)
 that represents the $PICKLE token. On [Etherscan](https://etherscan.io/tx/0x2bb7c8283b782355875fa37d05e4bd962519ea294678a3dcf2fdffbbd0761bc5#eventlog)
, the undecoded event looks like this:![Etherscan event log screenshot](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/images/etherscan.png)If we query for this transaction in the \`ethereum.logs\` table in the Dune database, we will receive the same encoded bytecode as our result dataset.

    SELECT *
    FROM ethereum.logs
    WHERE tx_hash = 0x2bb7c8283b782355875fa37d05e4bd962519ea294678a3dcf2fdffbbd0761bc5
    

We could make short work of this encoded bytecode by using [DuneSQL Varbinary functions](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/Functions-and-operators/varbinary)
 to decode it, but having the contract's ABI at hand makes this process much easier.  
This contract is decoded in Dune, so we can use the `pickle_finance_ethereum.PickleToken_evt_Transfer` table to access the decoded event log.

    SELECT *
    FROM pickle_finance_ethereum.PickleToken_evt_Transfer
    WHERE evt_tx_hash = 0x2bb7c8283b782355875fa37d05e4bd962519ea294678a3dcf2fdffbbd0761bc5

**Now this is actually useful for analyzing this transaction!** This data is much more readable and understandable than the encoded bytecode. We can see the sender, receiver, and the amount of tokens transferred in this event log.

How do I understand decoded data?
---------------------------------

Decoded data is the high level programming language representation of two pieces of software talking to each other via the blockchain.It's not always easy for a human to understand what exactly is going on in these interactions, but most of the time, looking at column names and the data that is transmitted within them should help you to understand what is happening within that specific log or call.If you are not able to make sense of the data by just searching the tables, it usually helps to look at single transactions using the transaction hash and [Etherscan](https://etherscan.io/)
.Furthermore, going into the code of the smart contract (our favorite way to do this is [DethCode](https://etherscan.deth.net/)
) to read the comments or the actual logic can help to understand the smart contract's emitted data.If that also doesn't lead to satisfactory results, scouring the relevant docs and GitHub of the project can lead you to the desired answers. Furthermore, talking to the developers and core community of a project can also help you to get an understanding of the smart contracts.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Raise issue](https://github.com/duneanalytics/dune-docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/overview)

[Traces](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/raw/traces)
[Henesys Call Tables](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/call-tables)

⌘I

# henesys.blocks - Dune Docs

[Skip to main content](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/raw/blocks#content-area)

[Dune Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=8344ffbb623f6875145727e13925a620)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/dune/2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo/logo/dune-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=2zcFQ4cOAgHOUIIo&q=85&s=54f1a9a73ae8fe5ec0235a2e52f9b870)](https://dune.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Raw

henesys.blocks

[Docs](https://docs.dune.com/home)
[Data Catalog](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/overview)
[API Reference](https://docs.dune.com/api-reference/overview/introduction)
[SQL Query Engine](https://docs.dune.com/query-engine/overview)
[Resources](https://docs.dune.com/resources/credits-billing/overview)

Table description
-----------------

The `henesys.blocks` table contains information about blocks in the henesys blockchain. A block is a collection of transactions that are hashed and added to the blockchain. Each block contains a reference to the previous block, known as the parent hash, and a timestamp. The table contains information about each block, such as the block number, the block hash, the block size, the number of transactions, and the gas used.

Column Descriptions
-------------------

Datatypes on Snowflake datashare are different in some cases, read more [here](https://docs.dune.com/datashare/datashare#datatypes)
.

Table Sample
------------

Examples
--------

### Show the most recent blocks

    SELECT
        number,
        hash, 
        size,
        gas_used
      FROM henesys.blocks
      ORDER BY number DESC
      LIMIT 10

### Show the number of blocks mined each day

    SELECT
        date_trunc('day', time) AS day,
        count(distinct number)
      FROM henesys.blocks
      GROUP BY day
      ORDER BY day DESC

### Show the number of transactions in each block

    SELECT
        number,
        count(*)
      FROM henesys.blocks
      GROUP BY 1 
      LIMIT 10

*   [Resources](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/overview#resources)
    

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/overview#what-is-henesys)

What is Henesys?
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Henesys is Avalanche’s Layer 1 blockchain that powers the NEXPACE ecosystem and the MapleStory Universe. Built by Nexon’s blockchain subsidiary, Henesys provides a secure, scalable platform for Web3 gaming, enabling player-owned economies, decentralized governance, and cross-chain interoperability through Chainlink’s CCIP integration.

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/overview#key-features)

Key Features
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Gaming-Focused Infrastructure**: Specialized blockchain for Web3 gaming and NFT ecosystems
*   **Avalanche L1**: Built on Avalanche for high performance and scalability
*   **Player-Owned Economies**: Enables true ownership of in-game assets through NFTs
*   **Fusion-Fission Model**: Dynamic NFT/item supply balancing mechanism
*   **Cross-Chain Interoperability**: Chainlink CCIP integration for secure NFT portability across games

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/overview#ecosystem-highlights)

Ecosystem Highlights
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   MapleStory Universe integration with blockchain technology
*   NFT minting and trading for in-game assets
*   Synergy Apps ecosystem with open APIs for third-party developers
*   Support for various gaming use cases including:
    *   In-game item tokenization
    *   Player-to-player trading
    *   Cross-game asset portability
    *   Prediction markets and dashboards
    *   Community-driven tooling

[​](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/overview#data-on-dune)

Data on Dune
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

--------\
\
Access to raw blockchain data including blocks, transactions, logs, and traces](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/raw/blocks)

------------\
\
Human-readable contract interactions and events](https://docs.dune.com/data-catalog/evm/henesys/decoded/overview)
